The patient, a 16-year-old boy from the Ambalavao district of Madagascar presented with fever, chills, and myalgia suggestive of malaria and was treated with quinine. Three days later, the appearance of a right inguinal bubo with high-grade fever (temperature of 41C), delirium, and prostration led to the diagnosis of plague. The bubo was punctured, and the patient was treated with twice-daily intramuscular injections of streptomycin (2 g per day for 4 days) and oral trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole (2g per day for 10 days). The patient recovered but had severe asthenia for more than a month. This strain is of biovar Orientalis.
